509 
510 inline cFont *NEW_CFONTCALIBRI72()
511 {
512  cImage *img = new cImage();
513  cLoadPNG(img, CFONTCALIBRI72_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONTCALIBRI72_BYTEARRAY));
514 
515  cFont *font = new cFont();
516  font->m_charset.m_base = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET_BASE;
517  font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
518  font->m_charset.m_width = CFONTCALIBRI72_WIDTH;
519  font->m_charset.m_height = CFONTCALIBRI72_HEIGHT;
520  font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET_PAGES;
521  for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
522  {
523  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i ];
524  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+1];
525  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+2];
526  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+3];
527  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+4];
528  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+5];
529  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+6];
530  font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONTCALIBRI72_CHARSET[8*i+7];
531  }
532  font->m_charset.preProcess();
533 
534  font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<cImage>(img));
535 
536  return (font);
537 }
